    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_220382168" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/220382168" />
    <a title="~Tina~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2594672-tina"><img alt="~Tina~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1411474324p2/2594672.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/220382168?book_show_action=true">Oct 07, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="~Tina~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="~Tina~" href="/user/show/2594672-tina">~Tina~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2594672-tina?shelf=own-copy">own-copy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2594672-tina?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2594672-tina?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2594672-tina?shelf=read-2012">read-2012</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2594672-tina?shelf=jennifer-rocks">jennifer-rocks</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer220382168" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer433878712677299722"><b>Cursed</b> is a story about a girl named Ember McWilliams. Two years ago she was in a car accident that took away her father and even her own life. But her naturally gifted three year old sister, Olivia, brought her back from the dead, but at a price. While Olivia can bring back any living thing that dies, Ember causes death by a simple touch. <br/>Two years later, their mother isn't right and is still feeling the effects after the lost of her husband, money is running out and Ember has to take care of O</span>
  <span id="freeText433878712677299722" style="display:none"><b>Cursed</b> is a story about a girl named Ember McWilliams. Two years ago she was in a car accident that took away her father and even her own life. But her naturally gifted three year old sister, Olivia, brought her back from the dead, but at a price. While Olivia can bring back any living thing that dies, Ember causes death by a simple touch. <br />Two years later, their mother isn't right and is still feeling the effects after the lost of her husband, money is running out and Ember has to take care of Olivia. Even at school things aren't easy. Once popular and social, Ember is now teased and ridiculed. Being called a freak and Frankenstein because of the scars that linger on her arms and stomach. She has to wear gloves to avoid accidentally killing someone and her once brown eyes has turned a pale sky blue. <br />After a horrific incident that lead to a guy from school dying from one touch of Ember's skin, Jonathan Cromwell decides to intervene, kidnapping her entire family and relocating them to a remote place where there are others with the same gifts. Among them is Hayden Cromwell, the mysterious boy who quotes Oscar Wilde and takes Ember's breath away.<br />They say that they want to help her. Help her family. But can she really trust these people? <br />But then again, what choice does she have...?<br /><br />It's official! JLA can't write a bad book. She's proven time and time again that she is simply fearless when it comes to her writing. I love the unique voices she gives to each and everyone of her characters. And Ember is one of them. <br />This is a very different book compared to the rest of Jennifer's stories, but I still loved it just the same. <br />The supernatural concept, while isn't exactly something new, still felt fresh and alive and entertaining to witness.<br /><br />I have to admit, there are only a few characters that I really liked. Olivia was a doll-face. Her voice may have been a little to mature for her age, but like it said, she has an old soul about her, which was believable. Her gift is somewhat creepy or maybe it seemed like that to me since she was just so little. <br />~I loved Ember. She's not a very trusting soul, but if you can't even trust yourself then how <i>do</i> you trust others? Her lack of faith could be frustrating at times but I still found it reasonable. Her gift was really heartbreaking to see her struggle with, but I really admired her strength, her passion, her spunk and then eventually her confidence once she started to gain control. I also adore the way she stood by her sister and her mother. <br />~But what really owned this book for me was Hayden. He was such an amazing character. He's thoughtful and understanding and kind and really sees Ember for who she truly is. He never gave up on her, always believed that she's more then her curse and wanted to be with her despite the fact that she has a killer touch.<br />Together these two really put a smile on my face. They have a beautiful connection and a chemistry that melted my insides. It wasn't all insta-love either. Friendship with attraction and then the inevitable pull to be together. Just the way I like it. Jennifer really knows how to draw her readers in with an irresistible love story. Those scenes were sizzling, sweet and very sexy.<br />~But sadly, as for the rest of the characters, well, I didn't really like them much due to the way they treated Ember.<br />She had such a hard time in her old school that I figured being in a home with other people like her that they would be welcoming and accepting. But it was the opposite. They made her feel anything but welcome, making it abundantly clear to her face that they want her gone and even went so far as to do certain things so she would get the message. And what's worse is that they were never really redeemed in the end.<br />Parker was okay, but he had such little scenes that it was hard to connect with him. And while Jonathan had a moment at the very end, I had a hard time trusting or liking his stern and determined ways. What happened to Adam also broke my heart a little. That felt so unfair. Hayden was the only one in that house that made it count.<br /><br />With that said, I still really loved this book. I love being in one of Jennifer worlds. She has an easy going and all consuming style that makes me sink into anything she writes. I love her flawed but real characters. I loved seeing their gifts in action. This had a lot of unexpected twist and turns that I never saw coming. It's not predictable and had me guessing and entertained till the very last page. <br />This reads like a stand alone, but there is enough room for a sequel, which I would totally read.<br /><br />Mysterious, consuming and gripping, Jennifer L Armentrout has done it again!<br /><br />Special thanks to Spencer Hill Press for sending me a copy for review!</span>
  <a data-text-id="433878712677299722" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lea (Between fantasy and reality)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lea (Between fantasy and reality)" href="/user/show/4723618-lea-between-fantasy-and-reality">Lea (Between fantasy and reality)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4723618-lea-between-fantasy-and-reality?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4723618-lea-between-fantasy-and-reality?shelf=made-me-cry">made-me-cry</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer283062936" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9266773449732479269"><a href='http://booklalaland.blogspot.com/2012/09/cursed-by-jennifer-l-armentrout.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Between fantasy and reality</a><br/><br/><br/>Jennifer L. Armentrout has done it again. The easiness with which this woman creates fantastic stories and memorable characters really shouldn’t surprise me anymore She wrote a novel with an interesting plot, swoon worthy love interest, kick-ass heroine, a hurricane of emotions and plenty of surprises thrown our way. Again. I really look forward to any book she writes and every time she announces a new book I am so excited that I get on my friends nerves. “Cursed” is r</span>
  <span id="freeText9266773449732479269" style="display:none"><a href="http://booklalaland.blogspot.com/2012/09/cursed-by-jennifer-l-armentrout.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Between fantasy and reality</a><br /><br /><br />Jennifer L. Armentrout has done it again. The easiness with which this woman creates fantastic stories and memorable characters really shouldn’t surprise me anymore She wrote a novel with an interesting plot, swoon worthy love interest, kick-ass heroine, a hurricane of emotions and plenty of surprises thrown our way. Again. I really look forward to any book she writes and every time she announces a new book I am so excited that I get on my friends nerves. “Cursed” is really an amazing novel and I couldn’t stop reading until I was finished. Ember and Hayden are an amazing book couple and I cant help but notice that most of my favorite fictional couples were the fruit of Jennifer´s imagination. The storyline with the “gifted” kids and a main character whose touch kills was told in a unique way it so sucks you right in and you wont be able to get away even after you finish reading. There was a lot of interesting situations, steamy scenes, surprising revelations and emotional rollacoasters. <br /><br />This book cemented Jennifer L. Armentrout´s place among my top 5 favorite authors and since her every book gets even better than the previous one I think she will stay there for a very long time. For everyone who still hasn’t read any of her books ( if there even are any out there) you should. You will be introduced to amazing stories, special and fascinating characters and situations that will take your breath away.<br /></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer416957106" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2104025976134360493">Two years ago Ember was killed in a car accident but her little sister, who has a mysterious gift brought her back to life. But when Ember came back something was wrong .Now everything she touches dies.<br/><br/>I was lured into reading this book by the blurb on the front cover.<br/> <br/>It said “Jennifer L. Armentrout is the Queen of creating novels with kick-butt heroines, drop-dread gorgeous guys, and loads of sexual tension...” <br/><br/>I say “Meh...”<br/><br/>First of all Ember never once kicked anyone’s butt. What she did do w</span>
  <span id="freeText2104025976134360493" style="display:none">Two years ago Ember was killed in a car accident but her little sister, who has a mysterious gift brought her back to life. But when Ember came back something was wrong .Now everything she touches dies.<br /><br />I was lured into reading this book by the blurb on the front cover.<br /> <br />It said “Jennifer L. Armentrout is the Queen of creating novels with kick-butt heroines, drop-dread gorgeous guys, and loads of sexual tension...” <br /><br />I say “Meh...”<br /><br />First of all Ember never once kicked anyone’s butt. What she did do was a lot of feeling sorry for herself, ineffectually pointing fingers and random people and alienating herself from others. In fact there was only one moment in the book where I actually liked her and that was when she was high on painkillers. <br /><br />And as for the drop dead gorgeous Hayden, well I'm not so sure what was so special about him. Except for the fact that Ember kept constantly mentioning how hot he was. Maybe it is just me but I find that it is a characters actions and words that make them attractive not a never end list of their physical attributes.<br /><br />This books story line was supposed to be an intriguing mystery, but the plot was very convoluted and at times incredibly slow. I am sure the author is planning on making this into a series but so many things at the end of this book made no sense at all. And because there was no real set up for the next book the whole experience was very unsatisfying.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="2104025976134360493" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2219689319" />

        rated it

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/16091275-cursed">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3957464-jenn?shelf=high-school-days">high-school-days</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3957464-jenn?shelf=paranormal-supernatural">paranormal-supernatural</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2219689319" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5866555699790297364">This one had a very X-Men feel to it. Ember McWilliams died in a car accident and then was brought back by her sister. But when she came back, she came back different - now her touch kills anything that comes into contact with it. Suddenly Ember finds herself living in a giant mansion with other kids who have gifts, but there's something not right.<br/><br/>I enjoyed this book. I felt really bad for Ember because here was a girl who died and lost her father in the same night. Now, she can't touch anyone, </span>
  <span id="freeText5866555699790297364" style="display:none">This one had a very X-Men feel to it. Ember McWilliams died in a car accident and then was brought back by her sister. But when she came back, she came back different - now her touch kills anything that comes into contact with it. Suddenly Ember finds herself living in a giant mansion with other kids who have gifts, but there's something not right.<br /><br />I enjoyed this book. I felt really bad for Ember because here was a girl who died and lost her father in the same night. Now, she can't touch anyone, including her five year old sister and her own mother acts like she doesn't exist. She was learning to deal when her life is uprooted again. I honestly don't know how shes so sane with all the feelings she has. <br /><br />The romance was a little awkward for me. While I liked Hayden, his feelings were a little immediate and intense regarding Ember. I liked how he was helping her and the only real person to stand up for her, but I never got the love connection sparks. I honestly thought this was a series and we would have more time to meet them, so imagine my surprise when it just ended.<br /><br />Overall, I enjoyed it. I wanted more, but what I got was fun. </span>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer7221958691357702564">Good, angsty YA... but not <i>great.</i><br/><br/>Has a '<a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11408650.The_Unbecoming_of_Mara_Dyer__Mara_Dyer___1_' title='The Unbecoming of Mara Dyer (Mara Dyer, #1) by Michelle Hodkin' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Unbecoming of Mara Dyer</a>' feel to it. I'll most likely continue the series, but I'm not in any great hurry. It certainly didn't hit me like the Lux series did. Cursed is still a solid YA read that's not totally obsessed with sex, I'd recommend it to like-minded readers.</span>
  <span id="freeText7221958691357702564" style="display:none">Good, angsty YA... but not <i>great.</i><br /><br />Has a '<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11408650.The_Unbecoming_of_Mara_Dyer__Mara_Dyer___1_" title="The Unbecoming of Mara Dyer (Mara Dyer, #1) by Michelle Hodkin" rel="nofollow noopener">The Unbecoming of Mara Dyer</a>' feel to it.           <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6594537-marie?shelf=favourite-series">favourite-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6594537-marie?shelf=different">different</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6594537-marie?shelf=awesome">awesome</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6594537-marie?shelf=cute">cute</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6594537-marie?shelf=loved">loved</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6594537-marie?shelf=death">death</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer278151264" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14613471638370622892">Another amazing book by Jennifer Armentrout, I wouldn't say I loved it as much as I love her half-blood and lux series but I don't think I could ever NOT enjoy one of her books. <br/><br/>I was fixated by this series when she released the first 2 chapters so I was eager to snap up this book and read more. I could not put it down. Once I started it was like I could think of nothing else. <br/><br/>The whole story had me second guessing from the beginning. I didn't know who to trust, who was innocent and who was the </span>
  <span id="freeText14613471638370622892" style="display:none">Another amazing book by Jennifer Armentrout, I wouldn't say I loved it as much as I love her half-blood and lux series but I don't think I could ever NOT enjoy one of her books. <br /><br />I was fixated by this series when she released the first 2 chapters so I was eager to snap up this book and read more. I could not put it down. Once I started it was like I could think of nothing else. <br /><br />The whole story had me second guessing from the beginning. I didn't know who to trust, who was innocent and who was the culprit. It was fresh, mysterious and unpredictable, everything I love in a book. <br /><br />I loved how Ember and Hayden were unique, it felt like they were the only two people on earth when they were together. <br /><br />The only issue I had was Ember hardly ever saw Olivia, and it made me sad. Especially that scene where she cries for Liz. It's like after only a few short days she would pick her over Ember who raised her. And at the beginning it was like they were so bonded and so close. I loved how they had each other and depended and comforted and loved each other unconditionally as is expected from a sister and it was like that closeness disappeared after they moved. I know I'm being petty but that is how I genuinely felt. <br /><br />I can't wait for the next installment, this was a gripping novel and was brilliant as one comes to expect from anything written by Jennifer L. Armentrout.</span>
  <a data-text-id="14613471638370622892" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

So, by the small description of her new book Cursed, I find it similar to the most swoontastic book on earth, Touch (Denazen #1). If after reading Cursed I see that its similar to any other book I'v read, I'm gonna stop reading Jennifer's bo</span>

So, by the small description of her new book Cursed, I find it similar to the most swoontastic book on earth, Touch (Denazen #1). If after reading Cursed I see that its similar to any other book I'v read, I'm gonna stop reading Jennifer's books coz I really dont like people who copy others work.</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('hBE6sVwJLOLB89TIKzcLL/nRG1KErd45YvBttR6oaRpFpHjSPoct/fH7D8CvjLcJh4z3OwLLddqqh10/br4RtQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('ZVnqvGzTAX53r6ejhuqvVBSGww6r7Z7Tu22AxldSiiWk7KjfDl0AYUenfKsCURNyatsvZy2LNTBzGrBMJ0Tyig==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer15939465961453852690">Hey Guys! Please note: I don't send out ARCs for review. If you're interested in reviewing a book of mine before release date, please contact the appropriate publisher. I also do NOT check my Goodreads email.<br/><br/>To email me, please use the below addy. <br/>jenniferlarmentrout@live.com<br/><br/># 1 New York Times and # 1 International Bestselling author Jennifer lives in Charles Town, West Virginia. All the rumors yo</span>
  <span id="freeText15939465961453852690" style="display:none">Hey Guys! Please note: I don't send out ARCs for review. If you're interested in reviewing a book of mine before release date, please contact the appropriate publisher. I also do NOT check my Goodreads email.<br /><br />To email me, please use the below addy. <br />jenniferlarmentrout@live.com<br /><br /># 1 New York Times and # 1 International Bestselling author Jennifer lives in Charles Town, West Virginia. All the rumors you’ve heard about her state aren’t true. When she’s not hard at work writing. she spends her time reading, watching really bad zombie movies, pretending to write, hanging out with her husband and her Jack Russell Loki. In early 2015, Jennifer was diagnosed with retinitis pigmentosa, a group of rare genetic disorders that involve a breakdown and death of cells in the retina, eventually resulting in loss of vision, among other complications. Due to this diagnosis, educating people on the varying degrees of blindness has become of passion of hers, right alongside writing, which she plans to do as long as she can. <br /><br />Her dreams of becoming an author started in algebra class, where she spent most of her time writing short stories….which explains her dismal grades in math. Jennifer writes young adult paranormal, science fiction, fantasy, and contemporary romance. She is published with Tor, HarperCollins Avon and William Morrow, Entangled Teen and Brazen, Disney/Hyperion and Harlequin Teen. Her Wicked Series has been optioned by PassionFlix. Jennifer has won numerous awards, including the 2013 Reviewers Choice Award for Wait for You, the 2015 Editor’s Pick for Fall With Me, and the 2014/2015 Moerser-Jugendbuch- Jury award for Obsidian. Her young adult romantic suspense novel DON’T LOOK BACK was a 2014 nominated Best in Young Adult Fiction by YALSA. Her adult romantic suspense novel TILL DEATH was a Amazon Editor’s Pick and iBook Book of the Month. Her young adult contemporary THE PROBLEM WITH FOREVER is a 2017 RITA Award Winner in Young Adult Fiction. She also writes Adult and New Adult contemporary and paranormal romance under the name J. Lynn. She is published by Entangled Brazen and HarperCollins.<br /><br />She is the owner of ApollyCon and The Origin Event, the successful annual events that features over hundred bestselling authors in Young Adult, New Adult, and Adult Fiction, panels, parties, and more.</span>
